 Easy loans and credit cards combined with a stable source of income over a particular period create a sham for financial stability
 kabhi-kabhi yah aapako lambey samay se lambit ichchhaaon ko puraa karne kii khatir udhaar lene ke liye prerit kar saktaa he
 Eventually you reach a situation where monthly expenses and loan installments exceed your monthly income
 hataash hokar aap phir adhik udhaar le lete hai
 If this vicious cycle continues, before you realize it, you are trapped in a debt trap
 kuch log naukari khone, vyavsaay main haani, parivaar main apatkaaleen chikitsa kharch yaa anya sankaton kii vajah se isamen funs jate hai or is kadar ulajh jate hai ki karj chukaana mushkil hota he
 However, a solution to this is always present
 sabase pehle aapako sthiti kii gambhirtha or tatkaal sudhaar ke mahatv ko samajhane kii aavashyaktaa he
 Rishi Mehra, CEO of Wishfin
com, says, "to maintain fair savings, you need to assess needs and reduce unnecessary expenses
 isse aapako samay par kist chukaane main madad milegi
 If you have savings that are equal to the outstanding debt, then use them better to pay off the debt
 ''duusari baat, yadi kai sroton se udhaar liya he, to aapako pataa hona chahie ki koun-sa karj chukaana praathamikta he
 Paying credit card dues and outstanding personal loans first should always be your priority, as they are available at a higher interest rate
 phir aap surakshit rin, jaise ki gold lone, car lone or sampatti ke evaj main rin ko chuktaa kar sakate hai, kyonki aamtaur par inaki byaaj dar kam hoti he
 If you do not have enough savings but have assets like property, gold or car, then you can take a loan at a lower interest in lieu of these things
 yah credit card bakaayaa jaise mahange karj ko chukaane main aapaki madad karegaa
 You can also ask lenders to extend the duration of secured loans
 isse iemi ghategi or aapke ke liye rin chukaana aasaan ho jayega
 If your income rises in the future, you can always repay the loan ahead of time
 yadi kam laagat vaala karj chukaane ke liye bhi aapaki aay paryaapt nahin he, lekin agar aapke paas sona, car jaisi parisampatti he, to use bechney main sankoch na karen
 As far as the property is occupied, experts caution for it
 fundamentum advyjar ke saajheedaar abhirup rishi salaah dete hai ki ''pehle apane kabje vaali achal sampatti kaa uchit moolyankan karen, phir faisla karen ki karj chukaane ke liye use bechnaa he yaa nahin
 Unless you have decided to buy a house or flat to live in, the decision to sell the occupied real estate is not right
 ''iske alaava, apane parijanon yaa doston se byaaj mukt karj maangane main sankoch nahin karen
 If none of the measures work, then finally contact the Credit Counseling Center, which specializes in getting people out of the debt trap
